            function isLightThemeSelected() {
                return document.cookie.match(/theme=light/i) != null
            }

            function setThemeFromCookie() {
                var html = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0]
                html.className = isLightThemeSelected() ? 'light-mode' : 'dark-mode'
                console.log('Loaded cookie: ' + document.cookie)
            }

            (function() {
              setThemeFromCookie()
            })();

<script>
moment.locale("en");
function flask_moment_render(elem) {{
    const timestamp = moment(elem.dataset.timestamp);
    const func = elem.dataset.function;
    const format = elem.dataset.format;
    const timestamp2 = elem.dataset.timestamp2;
    const no_suffix = elem.dataset.nosuffix;
    const units = elem.dataset.units;
    let args = [];
    if (format)
        args.push(format);
    if (timestamp2)
        args.push(moment(timestamp2));
    if (no_suffix)
        args.push(no_suffix);
    if (units)
        args.push(units);
    elem.textContent = timestamp[func].apply(timestamp, args);
    elem.classList.remove('flask-moment');
    elem.style.display = "";
}}
function flask_moment_render_all() {{
    const moments = document.querySelectorAll('.flask-moment');
    moments.forEach(function(moment) {{
        flask_moment_render(moment);
        const refresh = moment.dataset.refresh;
        if (refresh && refresh > 0) {{
            (function(elem, interval) {{
                setInterval(function() {{
                    flask_moment_render(elem);
                }}, interval);
            }})(moment, refresh);
        }}
    }})
}}
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", flask_moment_render_all);
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
    function updateThemeToggleFooter() {
      var elem = document.querySelector('#changeTheme');
      elem.innerHTML = isLightThemeSelected() ? 'Dark Mode' : 'Light Mode'
    }

    (function() {
      updateThemeToggleFooter()
    })();

    function togglePageContentLightDark() {
        var html = document.getElementsByTagName('html')[0]
        var currentClass = html.className
        var newClass = html.className == 'dark-mode' ? 'light-mode' : 'dark-mode'
        html.className = newClass

        document.cookie = 'theme=' + (newClass == 'light-mode' ? 'light' : 'dark') + ';SameSite=Strict;path=/;expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT'
        console.log('Cookies are now: ' + document.cookie)

        var elem = document.querySelector('#changeTheme');
        elem.innerHTML = isLightThemeSelected() ? 'Dark Mode' : 'Light Mode'
    }

    $("#changeTheme").on("click", function(e){
    togglePageContentLightDark();

    if ($("#darktheme").length) {
      if(isLightThemeSelected()){
        $('#darktheme').prop('checked', false);
        $('#lighttheme').prop('checked', true);
      }
      else{
        $('#darktheme').prop('checked', true);
        $('#lighttheme').prop('checked', false);
      }
    }
    });
    </script>

    <script>
      (function() {
        var weekly = document.getElementById("weekly-top-users");
        if (!weekly) return;
        fetch("/api/score/top")
          .then(function(r){ return r.json(); })
          .then(function(data) {
            var users = (data && data.users) ? data.users.slice(0, 5) : [];
            if (!users.length) {
              weekly.innerHTML = "<tr class='userrow visible row'><td class='col s12'>No scores yet.</td></tr>";
              return;
            }
            weekly.innerHTML = users.map(function(u, i) {
              return "<tr class='userrow visible row'>" +
                "<td class='col s4'>#" + (i+1) + "</td>" +
                "<td class='col s5'>" + u.name + "</td>" +
                "<td class='col s3'><i class='fas fa-star gold-text tooltipped' data-tooltip='Points'></i> " + u.score + "</td>" +
                "</tr>";
            }).join("");
          })
          .catch(function(){
            weekly.innerHTML = "<tr class='userrow visible row'><td class='col s12'>Failed to load.</td></tr>";
          });
      })();

      (function() {
        var recent = document.getElementById("recent-solves");
        if (!recent) return;
        fetch("/api/score/recent")
          .then(function(r){ return r.json(); })
          .then(function(data) {
            var solves = (data && data.solves) ? data.solves : [];
            if (!solves.length) {
              recent.innerHTML = "<tr class='userrow visible row'><td class='col s12'>No solves yet.</td></tr>";
              return;
            }
            recent.innerHTML = solves.map(function(s) {
              var when = new Date(s.ts || 0).toLocaleString();
              var title = s.name && s.name.length ? s.name : s.id;
              return "<tr class='userrow visible row'>" +
                "<td class='rank col s4'>" + title + "</td>" +
                "<td class='rank col s5'>" + s.user + "</td>" +
                "<td class='col s3'>" + when + "</td>" +
                "</tr>";
            }).join("");
          })
          .catch(function(){
            recent.innerHTML = "<tr class='userrow visible row'><td class='col s12'>Failed to load.</td></tr>";
          });
      })();

      (function() {
        function escapeHtml(text) {
          return String(text || "").replace(/[&<>"']/g, function(ch) {
            return ({ "&": "&amp;", "<": "&lt;", ">": "&gt;", '"': "&quot;", "'": "&#39;" })[ch];
          });
        }
        var registry = document.getElementById("registry-challenges");
        if (!registry) return;
        fetch("/api/challenges")
          .then(function(r){ return r.json(); })
          .then(function(data) {
            var challenges = (data && data.challenges) ? data.challenges.slice(0, 5) : [];
            if (!challenges.length) {
              registry.innerHTML = "<tr class='userrow visible row'><td class='col s12'>No live challenges yet.</td></tr>";
              return;
            }
            registry.innerHTML = challenges.map(function(ch) {
              return "<tr class='userrow visible row'>" +
                "<td class='col s4'>" + escapeHtml(ch.category) + "</td>" +
                "<td class='col s5'><a href='challenge/index.html?id=" + encodeURIComponent(ch.id) + "'>" + escapeHtml(ch.title) + "</a></td>" +
                "<td class='col s3'>" + escapeHtml(ch.points) + " pts</td>" +
                "</tr>";
            }).join("");
          })
          .catch(function(){
            registry.innerHTML = "<tr class='userrow visible row'><td class='col s12'>Failed to load.</td></tr>";
          });
      })();
    </script>

//# sourceMappingURL=/sm/bf47ebc07e6c6098c39b6e8d68bf830f3f6f1fbf710de77e3981b8b8bc4e9315.map

/* ==== https://ctf.a4xinjector.in/static/js/api.js ==== */
var api = (function() {
    var makeCall = function(endpoint, data, callback) {
        $.ajax({
            url: "/api" + endpoint,
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            method: "POST",
            success: function(data) {
                console.log(data);
                callback(data);
                console.log("API call complete");
            },
            error: function(xhr, status, err) {
                console.error("API call failed", status, err);
            }
        });
    };

    var makeCallGet = function(endpoint, data, callback) {
        $.ajax({
            url: "/api" + endpoint,
            data: data,
            dataType: "json",
            method: "GET",
            success: function(data) {
                console.log(data);
                callback(data);
                console.log("API call complete");
            },
            error: function(xhr, status, err) {
                console.error("API call failed", status, err);
            }
        });
    };

    return {
        makeCall: makeCall,
        makeCallGet: makeCallGet
    };
})();

// Static-site safe defaults for challenge submit flow
if (typeof window !== "undefined") {
    function getSiteRootUrl() {
        // Prefer the page's logo link (already correct relative path).
        var logo = document.querySelector("a.logo-link");
        var href = logo ? (logo.getAttribute("href") || "") : "";
        try {
            if (href) return new URL(href, window.location.href).href;
        } catch (e) {}
        try {
            return new URL("index.html", window.location.href).href;
        } catch (e) {}
        return "/index.html";
    }

    function findSideNav() {
        // Mobile uses the element with id="nav-mobile"; some pages also have the
        // "fixed" class for desktop. Prefer the id, then fall back.
        return (
            document.getElementById("nav-mobile") ||
            document.querySelector("ul.side-nav.fixed") ||
            document.querySelector("ul.side-nav")
        );
    }

    function findTopNav() {
        return document.querySelector("nav .nav-wrapper ul.right.hide-on-med-and-down");
    }

    function shouldEnableWormCursor() {
        // Cursor effects don't make sense on touch devices and can break UX.
        try {
            if (window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia("(pointer: coarse)").matches) return false;
            if (window.matchMedia && !window.matchMedia("(pointer: fine)").matches) return false;
        } catch (e) {}

        var p = (window.location && window.location.pathname) ? window.location.pathname : "";
        p = String(p || "").toLowerCase();

        // Never enable on these sections.
        if (p.indexOf("/courses") !== -1) return false;
        if (p.indexOf("/challenges") !== -1) return false;

        // Allowlist "important" pages only (keeps the rest calm).
        if (p === "/" || p.endsWith("/index.html")) return true;
        if (p.indexOf("/scoreboard") !== -1) return true;
        if (p.indexOf("/profile") !== -1) return true;
        if (p.indexOf("/admin") !== -1) return true;
        if (p.indexOf("/login") !== -1) return true;
        if (p.indexOf("/register") !== -1) return true;

        return false;
    }

    function initWormCursor() {
        if (!shouldEnableWormCursor()) return;
        if (window.__wormCursorInit) return;
        window.__wormCursorInit = true;

        // CSS for hiding the cursor + node styling lives in static/css/main77ae.css.
        try {
            document.documentElement.classList.add("worm-cursor");
        } catch (e) {}

        var numNodes = 18;
        var nodes = [];

        for (var i = 0; i < numNodes; i++) {
            var node = document.createElement("div");
            node.className = "worm-node" + (i === 0 ? " head" : "");
            node.textContent = Math.random() > 0.5 ? "1" : "0";
            node.style.opacity = String(1 - i / numNodes);
            document.body.appendChild(node);
            nodes.push({
                el: node,
                x: -100,
                y: -100,
                sc: 1 - (i / numNodes) * 0.55
            });
        }

        var mouseX = -1000;
        var mouseY = -1000;
        var isActive = false;

        document.addEventListener("mousemove", function(e) {
            mouseX = e.clientX;
            mouseY = e.clientY;
        });

        function animate() {
            var spring = isActive ? 0.62 : 0.32;

            nodes[0].x += (mouseX - nodes[0].x) * spring;
            nodes[0].y += (mouseY - nodes[0].y) * spring;
            nodes[0].el.style.transform =
                "translate3d(" + nodes[0].x + "px," + nodes[0].y + "px,0) scale(" + nodes[0].sc + ")";

            for (var j = 1; j < nodes.length; j++) {
                nodes[j].x += (nodes[j - 1].x - nodes[j].x) * spring;
                nodes[j].y += (nodes[j - 1].y - nodes[j].y) * spring;
                nodes[j].el.style.transform =
                    "translate3d(" + nodes[j].x + "px," + nodes[j].y + "px,0) scale(" + nodes[j].sc + ")";

                if (Math.random() > 0.96) nodes[j].el.textContent = Math.random() > 0.5 ? "1" : "0";
            }

            window.requestAnimationFrame(animate);
        }

        window.requestAnimationFrame(animate);

        // Speed up when hovering interactive elements.
        try {
            var sel = "a, button, input, textarea, select, .btn, .ledger-row, .feat-item";
            document.querySelectorAll(sel).forEach(function(el) {
                el.addEventListener("mouseenter", function() { isActive = true; });
                el.addEventListener("mouseleave", function() { isActive = false; });
            });
        } catch (e) {}
    }

    function applyStoredTheme() {
        var stored = null;
        try {
            stored = localStorage.getItem("site-theme");
        } catch (e) {}
        if (!stored) return;
        var html = document.documentElement;
        html.className = stored === "light" ? "light-mode" : "dark-mode";
    }

    function wrapThemeToggle() {
        if (!window.togglePageContentLightDark || window.__themeWrapped) return;
        var original = window.togglePageContentLightDark;
        window.togglePageContentLightDark = function() {
            original.apply(this, arguments);
            try {
                var cls = document.documentElement.className;
                localStorage.setItem("site-theme", cls === "light-mode" ? "light" : "dark");
            } catch (e) {}
        };
        window.__themeWrapped = true;
    }

    function isAuthLink(anchor, kind) {
        if (!anchor) return false;
        var href = (anchor.getAttribute("href") || "").toLowerCase();
        // Matches "register/", "../register/", "register/index.html", etc.
        if (kind === "register") return /(^|\/)register(\/|\/index\.html)?$/.test(href) || href.indexOf("/register/") !== -1;
        if (kind === "login") return /(^|\/)login(\/|\/index\.html)?$/.test(href) || href.indexOf("/login/") !== -1;
        return false;
    }

    function setLiVisible(li, visible) {
        if (!li) return;
        li.style.display = visible ? "" : "none";
    }

    function setManyVisible(items, visible) {
        if (!items || !items.length) return;
        items.forEach(function(li) {
            setLiVisible(li, visible);
        });
    }

    function ensureNavItem(nav, id, href, iconClass, text, onClick) {
        if (!nav) return null;
        var existing = nav.querySelector('li[data-auth-item="' + id + '"]');
        if (existing) {
            var a0 = existing.querySelector("a");
            if (a0) a0.setAttribute("href", href);
            return existing;
        }

        var li = document.createElement("li");
        li.setAttribute("data-auth-item", id);

        var a = document.createElement("a");
        a.setAttribute("href", href);

        var sideIcon = document.createElement("div");
        sideIcon.className = "side-icon";
        var i = document.createElement("i");
        i.className = iconClass;
        sideIcon.appendChild(i);

        var sideText = document.createElement("div");
        sideText.className = "side-text";
        sideText.textContent = text;

        a.appendChild(sideIcon);
        a.appendChild(sideText);
        li.appendChild(a);

        if (typeof onClick === "function") {
            a.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                onClick(e);
            });
        }

        // Insert near the top of the nav, after the existing auth links if present.
        var insertBefore = null;
        var lis = nav.querySelectorAll("li");
        for (var idx = 0; idx < lis.length; idx++) {
            var link = lis[idx].querySelector("a");
            if (link && (isAuthLink(link, "register") || isAuthLink(link, "login"))) {
                insertBefore = lis[idx].nextSibling;
            }
        }
        nav.insertBefore(li, insertBefore);
        return li;
    }

    function ensureTopNavItem(nav, id, href, text, onClick) {
        if (!nav) return null;
        var existing = nav.querySelector('li[data-auth-top="' + id + '"]');
        if (existing) {
            var a0 = existing.querySelector("a");
            if (a0) a0.setAttribute("href", href);
            return existing;
        }

        var li = document.createElement("li");
        li.setAttribute("data-auth-top", id);

        var a = document.createElement("a");
        a.setAttribute("href", href);
        a.textContent = text;
        li.appendChild(a);

        if (typeof onClick === "function") {
            a.addEventListener("click", function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                onClick(e);
            });
        }

        nav.appendChild(li);
        return li;
    }

    async function updateAuthNav() {
        var nav = findSideNav();
        var topNav = findTopNav();
        if (!nav && !topNav) return;

        var siteRoot = getSiteRootUrl(); // usually .../index.html
        var profileUrl = "";
        try {
            profileUrl = new URL("profile/index.html", siteRoot).href;
        } catch (e) {
            profileUrl = "profile/index.html";
        }

        var loginUrl = "";
        var registerUrl = "";
        try {
            loginUrl = new URL("login/index.html", siteRoot).href;
            registerUrl = new URL("register/index.html", siteRoot).href;
        } catch (e) {}

        var me = null;
        try {
            var res = await fetch("/api/auth/me", { method: "GET", credentials: "include" });
            me = await res.json().catch(function() { return null; });
        } catch (e) {}

        var loggedIn = !!(me && me.logged_in && me.user);
        var roles = (loggedIn && me.user && Array.isArray(me.user.roles)) ? me.user.roles : [];
        var isAdminRole = roles.indexOf("owner") !== -1 ||
            roles.indexOf("admin") !== -1 ||
            roles.indexOf("moderator") !== -1 ||
            roles.indexOf("author") !== -1 ||
            roles.indexOf("analyst") !== -1;

        // Find all existing register/login items (some pages include duplicates).
        var registerLis = [];
        var loginLis = [];
        if (nav) {
            nav.querySelectorAll("li").forEach(function(li) {
                var a = li.querySelector("a");
                if (!a) return;
                if (isAuthLink(a, "register")) registerLis.push(li);
                if (isAuthLink(a, "login")) loginLis.push(li);
            });
        }

        var topRegisterLis = [];
        var topLoginLis = [];
        if (topNav) {
            topNav.querySelectorAll("li").forEach(function(li) {
                var a = li.querySelector("a");
                if (!a) return;
                if (isAuthLink(a, "register")) topRegisterLis.push(li);
                if (isAuthLink(a, "login")) topLoginLis.push(li);
            });
        }

        if (!loggedIn) {
            // Ensure register/login are visible.
            setManyVisible(registerLis, true);
            setManyVisible(loginLis, true);
            setManyVisible(topRegisterLis, true);
            setManyVisible(topLoginLis, true);

            // Ensure desktop top-nav has login/register even if missing.
            if (topNav && loginUrl) {
                var tLogin = ensureTopNavItem(topNav, "login", loginUrl, "Login");
                setLiVisible(tLogin, true);
            }
            if (topNav && registerUrl) {
                var tReg = ensureTopNavItem(topNav, "register", registerUrl, "Create Account");
                setLiVisible(tReg, true);
            }

            // Remove/hide profile/logout if present.
            var p = nav ? nav.querySelector('li[data-auth-item="profile"]') : null;
            var lo = nav ? nav.querySelector('li[data-auth-item="logout"]') : null;
            var adminItem = nav ? nav.querySelector('li[data-auth-item="admin"]') : null;
            setLiVisible(p, false);
            setLiVisible(lo, false);
            setLiVisible(adminItem, false);

            var tp = topNav ? topNav.querySelector('li[data-auth-top="profile"]') : null;
            var tlo = topNav ? topNav.querySelector('li[data-auth-top="logout"]') : null;
            var tadm = topNav ? topNav.querySelector('li[data-auth-top="admin"]') : null;
            setLiVisible(tp, false);
            setLiVisible(tlo, false);
            setLiVisible(tadm, false);
            return;
        }

        // Sync scoreboard display name to logged-in username.
        try {
            if (me.user && me.user.username) localStorage.setItem("player-name", me.user.username);
        } catch (e) {}

        // Hide register/login when logged in.
        setManyVisible(registerLis, false);
        setManyVisible(loginLis, false);
        setManyVisible(topRegisterLis, false);
        setManyVisible(topLoginLis, false);

        // Add Profile and Logout entries.
        if (nav) {
            var profileLi = ensureNavItem(nav, "profile", profileUrl, "fas fa-user", "Profile");
            setLiVisible(profileLi, true);
        }

        if (topNav) {
            var topProfileLi = ensureTopNavItem(topNav, "profile", profileUrl, "Profile");
            setLiVisible(topProfileLi, true);
        }

        var adminUrl = "";
        try {
            adminUrl = new URL("admin/index.html", siteRoot).href;
        } catch (e) {
            adminUrl = "admin/index.html";
        }

        if (isAdminRole) {
            if (nav) {
                var adminLi = ensureNavItem(nav, "admin", adminUrl, "fas fa-shield-alt", "Admin");
                setLiVisible(adminLi, true);
            }
            if (topNav) {
                var topAdminLi = ensureTopNavItem(topNav, "admin", adminUrl, "Admin");
                setLiVisible(topAdminLi, true);
            }
        }

        var doLogout = async function() {
            try {
                await fetch("/api/auth/logout", { method: "POST", credentials: "include" });
            } catch (e) {}
            try {
                localStorage.removeItem("player-name");
            } catch (e) {}
            // Go back to the site root and reload to ensure nav updates.
            try {
                window.location.href = siteRoot;
            } catch (e) {
                window.location.reload();
            }
        };

        if (nav) {
            var logoutLi = ensureNavItem(
                nav,
                "logout",
                "#logout",
                "fas fa-sign-out-alt",
                "Logout",
                doLogout
            );
            setLiVisible(logoutLi, true);
        }

        if (topNav) {
            var topLogoutLi = ensureTopNavItem(topNav, "logout", "#logout", "Logout", doLogout);
            setLiVisible(topLogoutLi, true);
        }

        // If some pages have hard-coded login/register URLs and we computed better ones,
        // update them (keeps navigation consistent after our link rewrites).
        if (loginUrl && loginLis.length) {
            loginLis.forEach(function(li) {
                var a = li.querySelector("a");
                if (a) a.setAttribute("href", loginUrl);
            });
        }
        if (registerUrl && registerLis.length) {
            registerLis.forEach(function(li) {
                var a = li.querySelector("a");
                if (a) a.setAttribute("href", registerUrl);
            });
        }

        // Sync desktop top-nav login/register hrefs too (if they exist).
        if (topNav) {
            if (loginUrl && topLoginLis.length) {
                topLoginLis.forEach(function(li) {
                    var a = li.querySelector("a");
                    if (a) a.setAttribute("href", loginUrl);
                });
            }
            if (registerUrl && topRegisterLis.length) {
                topRegisterLis.forEach(function(li) {
                    var a = li.querySelector("a");
                    if (a) a.setAttribute("href", registerUrl);
                });
            }
        }
    }

    if (typeof window.score === "undefined") {
        window.score = 0;
    }
    if (typeof window.calculateLevel === "undefined") {
        window.calculateLevel = function(score, points) {
            score = score || 0;
            points = points || 0;
            return score + points;
        };
    }
    if (typeof window.showCorrectToast === "undefined") {
        window.showCorrectToast = function(message) {
            if (window.Materialize && typeof Materialize.toast === "function") {
                Materialize.toast(message || "Correct!", 4000, "green");
            }
        };
    }
    if (typeof window.handleCorrectFlag === "undefined") {
        window.handleCorrectFlag = function(id) {
            if (!id) return;
            try {
                localStorage.setItem("solved-" + id, "1");
            } catch (e) {}
            try {
                sessionStorage.removeItem("a4x_scoreboard_cache");
            } catch (e) {}
            window.showCorrectToast("Correct!");
            if (window.updateScoreboard) {
                window.updateScoreboard(id);
            }
        };
    }
    if (typeof window.applySolvedState === "undefined") {
        window.applySolvedState = function() {
            var forms = document.querySelectorAll("form[data-challenge]");
            forms.forEach(function(form) {
                var id = form.getAttribute("data-challenge");
                if (!id) return;
                var solved = false;
                try {
                    solved = localStorage.getItem("solved-" + id) === "1";
                } catch (e) {}
                if (!solved) return;
                var uncheck = document.getElementById("uncheck-" + id);
                var check = document.getElementById("check-" + id);
                if (uncheck) uncheck.style.display = "none";
                if (check) check.style.display = "";
                form.style.display = "none";
                var youSolved = document.getElementById("youvesolved-" + id);
                if (youSolved) youSolved.style.display = "";
            });
        };
    }
    function initLazyImages() {
        document.querySelectorAll("img").forEach(function(img) {
            if (!img.hasAttribute("loading")) img.setAttribute("loading", "lazy");
        });
    }

    applyStoredTheme();
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        if (window.applySolvedState) window.applySolvedState();
        wrapThemeToggle();
        initLazyImages();
        // Auth-aware sidebar entries (Profile/Logout vs Login/Register).
        updateAuthNav();
        // Materialize may initialize/clone the sidenav after DOMContentLoaded on mobile.
        setTimeout(updateAuthNav, 300);
        setTimeout(wrapThemeToggle, 500);
        initWormCursor();
    });

    if (typeof window.getPlayerName === "undefined") {
        window.getPlayerName = function() {
            var name = null;
            try {
                name = localStorage.getItem("player-name");
            } catch (e) {}
            if (name) return name;
            name = prompt("Enter a display name for the scoreboard:");
            if (!name) return null;
            name = name.trim().slice(0, 24);
            if (!name) return null;
            try {
                localStorage.setItem("player-name", name);
            } catch (e) {}
            return name;
        };
    }

    if (typeof window.updateScoreboard === "undefined") {
        window.updateScoreboard = async function(id) {
            var form = document.getElementById("flagform-" + id);
            if (!form) {
                form = document.querySelector('form[data-challenge="' + id + '"]');
            }
            if (!form) {
                form = document.getElementById("flag-form");
            }
            if (!form) return;
            var points = parseInt(form.getAttribute("data-points") || "0", 10) || 0;
            var name = null;
            var header = document.getElementById("header-" + id);
            if (header) {
                var text = header.querySelector(".challenge-text");
                if (text) name = text.textContent.trim();
            }
            if (!name) {
                var title = document.getElementById("challenge-title");
                if (title) name = (title.textContent || "").trim();
            }
            var user = window.getPlayerName();
            if (!user) return;
            try {
                var res = await fetch("/api/score/add", {
                    method: "POST",
                    headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
                    credentials: "include",
                    body: JSON.stringify({ user: user, id: id, name: name, points: points })
                });
                var data = await res.json().catch(function() { return {}; });
                if (!res.ok) {
                    if (data && data.error && window.Materialize && typeof Materialize.toast === "function") {
                        Materialize.toast(data.error, 4000);
                    }
                    return;
                }
                try {
                    sessionStorage.removeItem("a4x_scoreboard_cache");
                } catch (e) {}
            } catch (e) {}
        };
    }
}
